## Risks that can be mitigated by this stakeholder

* [33% of works do not identify pandemic disruptions](https://github.com/mm80843/T3.5/blob/pages/Risk/PBN__Risk_1050.md)
* [35 cohort studies and 69 cross-sectional studies, including 18 large scale ecological studies, may increase the risk of disease transmission due to the close contact and interactions among participants.](https://github.com/mm80843/T3.5/blob/pages/Risk/PBN__Risk_1434.md)
* [A significant fraction of cases may go undetected with current testing algorithms, especially asymptomatic individuals.](https://github.com/mm80843/T3.5/blob/pages/Risk/PBN__Risk_1614.md)
* [Absence of a paper-based device to detect sars-cov-2 in wastewaters increases the risk of undetected viral presence in the environment and potential transmission.](https://github.com/mm80843/T3.5/blob/pages/Risk/PBN__Risk_1613.md)
* [Absence of approved therapy for covid-19](https://github.com/mm80843/T3.5/blob/pages/Risk/PBN__Risk_1036.md)
* [Absence of covid-19 treatment and delayed availability of vaccine](https://github.com/mm80843/T3.5/blob/pages/Risk/PBN__Risk_1301.md)
* [Accumulation of extraneous nucleic acids during the concentration process of wastewater samples.](https://github.com/mm80843/T3.5/blob/pages/Risk/PBN__Risk_2296.md)
* [Accurate forecasting of virus](https://github.com/mm80843/T3.5/blob/pages/Risk/PBN__Risk_1733.md)

* [Anonymous surveys used for evaluation may inadvertently collect sensitive personal data.](https://github.com/mm80843/T3.5/blob/pages/Risk/PBN__Risk_1480.md)
